3.3.4.evProthat⟨x⟩→⟨x⟩+dx′,⟨p⟩→⟨p⟩underinifnitesimaltranslation.

pectationaluevofsystembeforetranslationis⟨x⟩=⟨α|x|α⟩.Theexpectationaluevaftertranslation
